2) Работа  с архивированием и разархивированием файлов с помощью tar и gzip


vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  OutPut.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ tar -cvf myfirstTar.tar InPut.txt OutPut.txt 
InPut.txt
OutPut.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ tar -cvf thesecond.tar dir1 DIR1
dir1/
dir1/dir15
dir1/dir13
dir1/dir14
dir1/file.txt
dir1/dir12
dir1/dir11
DIR1/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ mkdir unPacking
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cd unPacking/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ cd ..
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ gzip thesecond.tar 
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar.gz  unPacking
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cd unPacking/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ tar -xvf ../thesecond.tar.gz 
dir1/
dir1/dir15
dir1/dir13
dir1/dir14
dir1/file.txt
dir1/dir12
dir1/dir11
DIR1/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ ls
dir1  DIR1

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ cd ..
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar.gz  unPacking
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ mv unPacking ./Folder
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  Folder  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar.gz
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ tar -cvzf tarOFtars.gz myfirstTar.tar thesecond.tar.gz
myfirstTar.tar
thesecond.tar.gz
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  Folder  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  tarOFtars.gz  thesecond.tar.gz
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ rm myfirstTar.tar thesecond.tar.gz 
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  Folder  from_sftp  InPut.txt  OutPut.txt  tarOFtars.gz
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls -la

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111

/usr/bin/bash

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ unset name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ unset name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls

OutPut.txt

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ unset name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export

2) Работа  с архивированием и разархивированием файлов с помощью tar и gzip


vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  OutPut.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ tar -cvf myfirstTar.tar InPut.txt OutPut.txt 
InPut.txt
OutPut.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ tar -cvf thesecond.tar dir1 DIR1
dir1/
dir1/dir15
dir1/dir13
dir1/dir14
dir1/file.txt
dir1/dir12
dir1/dir11
DIR1/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ mkdir unPacking
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cd unPacking/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ cd ..
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ gzip thesecond.tar 
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar.gz  unPacking
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cd unPacking/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ tar -xvf ../thesecond.tar.gz 
dir1/
dir1/dir15
dir1/dir13
dir1/dir14
dir1/file.txt
dir1/dir12
dir1/dir11
DIR1/

dir1  DIR1

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ cd ..
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls

myfirstTar.tar
thesecond.tar.gz

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ unset name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ unset name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export

2) Работа  с архивированием и разархивированием файлов с помощью tar и gzip


vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  OutPut.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ tar -cvf myfirstTar.tar InPut.txt OutPut.txt 
InPut.txt
OutPut.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ tar -cvf thesecond.tar dir1 DIR1
dir1/
dir1/dir15
dir1/dir13
dir1/dir14
dir1/file.txt
dir1/dir12
dir1/dir11
DIR1/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ mkdir unPacking
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cd unPacking/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ cd ..
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ gzip thesecond.tar 
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar.gz  unPacking
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cd unPacking/
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ tar -xvf ../thesecond.tar.gz 
dir1/
dir1/dir15
dir1/dir13
dir1/dir14
dir1/file.txt
dir1/dir12
dir1/dir11
DIR1/

dir1  DIR1

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex/unPacking$ cd ..
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ mv unPacking ./Folder
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ ls
dir1  DIR1  Folder  from_sftp  InPut.txt  myfirstTar.tar  OutPut.txt  thesecond.tar.gz
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ tar -cvzf tarOFtars.gz myfirstTar.tar thesecond.tar.gz
myfirstTar.tar
thesecond.tar.gz

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ unset name

4) Переменные, $ $() $(())

vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num1=777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
1
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1
777
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ plus=+
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ num2=223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2
777 + 223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $num1 $plus $num2|bc >> SOMEfile.txt
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ cat SOMEfile.txt 
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export globalVAR="Hello, world!"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $globalVAR 
Hello, world!
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$num1+$num2
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo res
res
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
777+223
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$($num1+$num2)
777+223: команда не найдена
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res=$(($num1+$num2))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res
1000
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ res2=$(($res+111))
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $res2
1111
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH
/usr/bin/bash
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $BASH_VERSION 
5.1.16(1)-release
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
17880
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
4174
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $RANDOM 
5092
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $OSTYPE
linux-gnu
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $USER
vadim
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ name='Tom'
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo "Welcome, $name"
Welcome, Tom
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo 'Welcome, $name'
Welcome, $name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ echo $?
0
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ export name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
name=Tom	//env - выводит все переменные среды, нужно делать export
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ unset name
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$ env|grep "name"
vadim@vadim-GF65-Thin-9SEXR:~/ex$
